# Get the draft content of the contract with user details parsed - FirstPromoter Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-affiliate/contract-documents/get-the-draft-content-of-the-contract-with-user-details-parsed#content-area)

[FirstPromoter Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/firstpromoter/HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL&q=85&s=6ded212b82547bec37a22e90f72eeb71)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/firstpromoter/HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL&q=85&s=c393ff83772047b8a444f78a1e393e7f)](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/)

[Affiliate API Reference](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-affiliate/introduction)

Get the draft content of the contract

cURL

Copy

    curl --request POST \
      --url https://api.firstpromoter.com/api/v2/affiliate/contract_documents/draft \
      --header 'Account-ID: <account-id>' \
      --header 'Authorization: Bearer <token>' \
      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      --data '
    {
      "contract_id": 123,
      "details": {
        "email": "<string>",
        "profile": {
          "first_name": "<string>"
        }
      }
    }
    '

200

404

Copy

    {
      "content": "<string>"
    }

POST

/

contract\_documents

/

draft

Try it

Get the draft content of the contract

cURL

Copy

    curl --request POST \
      --url https://api.firstpromoter.com/api/v2/affiliate/contract_documents/draft \
      --header 'Account-ID: <account-id>' \
      --header 'Authorization: Bearer <token>' \
      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      --data '
    {
      "contract_id": 123,
      "details": {
        "email": "<string>",
        "profile": {
          "first_name": "<string>"
        }
      }
    }
    '

200

404

Copy

    {
      "content": "<string>"
    }

#### Authorizations

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-affiliate/contract-documents/get-the-draft-content-of-the-contract-with-user-details-parsed#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Access token passed as a Bearer token in the Authorization header

#### Headers

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-affiliate/contract-documents/get-the-draft-content-of-the-contract-with-user-details-parsed#parameter-account-id)

Account-ID

string

required

Account identifier that specifies which account is making the request

Example:

`"acc_123456"`

#### Body

application/json

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-affiliate/contract-documents/get-the-draft-content-of-the-contract-with-user-details-parsed#body-contract-id)

contract\_id

integer

ID of the contract

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-affiliate/contract-documents/get-the-draft-content-of-the-contract-with-user-details-parsed#body-details)

details

object

User details to parse

Show child attributes

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-affiliate/contract-documents/get-the-draft-content-of-the-contract-with-user-details-parsed#body-details-email)

details.email

string

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-affiliate/contract-documents/get-the-draft-content-of-the-contract-with-user-details-parsed#body-details-profile)

details.profile

object

Show child attributes

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-affiliate/contract-documents/get-the-draft-content-of-the-contract-with-user-details-parsed#body-details-profile-first-name)

details.profile.first\_name

string

#### Response

200

application/json

Draft content

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-affiliate/contract-documents/get-the-draft-content-of-the-contract-with-user-details-parsed#response-content)

content

string

Sign a document with id

cURL

Copy

    curl --request POST \
      --url https://api.firstpromoter.com/api/v2/affiliate/contract_documents/{id}/sign \
      --header 'Account-ID: <account-id>' \
      --header 'Authorization: Bearer <token>' \
      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      --data '
    {
      "ip": "<string>"
    }
    '

200

400

403

404

Copy

    {
      "id": 123,
      "status": "signed",
      "signed_ip": "<string>",
      "contract_version_id": 123,
      "signed_at": "2023-11-07T05:31:56Z",
      "promoter": {
        "id": 123,
        "email": "<string>",
        "name": "<string>",
        "profile": {
          "avatar": "<string>"
        }
      },
      "contract_version": {
        "added_at": "2023-11-07T05:31:56Z",
        "changes_made": "<string>",
        "external_link": "<string>",
        "content_hosted": true
      },
      "contract": {
        "id": 123,
        "name": "<string>"
      }
    }

`"acc_123456"`

Get affiliate email settings

cURL

Copy

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://api.firstpromoter.com/api/v2/affiliate/email_settings \
      --header 'Account-ID: <account-id>' \
      --header 'Authorization: Bearer <token>'

200

401

403

Copy

    {
      "data": [\
        {\
          "id": 123,\
          "company_domain": "<string>",\
          "emails_opt_drip": true,\
          "emails_opt_new_commission": true,\
          "emails_opt_new_referral": true,\
          "emails_opt_payout": true,\
          "company_name": "<string>",\
          "marketing_consent": true\
        }\
      ],
      "meta": {
        "email": "<string>"
      }
    }

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-affiliate/payout-methods/get-all-payout-methods-for-current-promoter#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Access token passed as a Bearer token in the Authorization header

#### Headers

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-affiliate/payout-methods/get-all-payout-methods-for-current-promoter#parameter-account-id)

string

required

Account identifier that specifies which account is making the request

Example:

`"acc_123456"`

Create a payout method

cURL

Copy

    curl --request POST \
      --url https://api.firstpromoter.com/api/v2/affiliate/payout_methods \
      --header 'Account-ID: <account-id>' \
      --header 'Authorization: Bearer <token>' \
      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      --data '
    {
      "method": "paypal",
      "details": {
        "paypal_email": "<string>",
        "wise_email": "<string>",
        "wallet_address": "<string>",
        "crypto_currency": "<string>",
        "bank_country": "AD",
        "account_holder_name": "<string>",
        "account_number": "<string>",
        "routing_aba_number": "<string>",
        "country": "<string>",
        "state": "<string>",
        "postal_code": "<string>",
        "address": "<string>",
        "city": "<string>",
        "transit_number": "<string>",
        "institution_number": "<string>",
        "bsb_code": "<string>",
        "sort_code": "<string>",
        "iban": "<string>",
        "swift_bic_code": "<string>",
        "bank_name": "<string>",
        "bank_city": "<string>",
        "bank_address": "<string>"
      },
      "is_disabled": true,
      "is_selected": true
    }
    '

Update a payout method

cURL

Copy

    curl --request PUT \
      --url https://api.firstpromoter.com/api/v2/affiliate/payout_methods/{id} \
      --header 'Account-ID: <account-id>' \
      --header 'Authorization: Bearer <token>' \
      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      --data '
    {
      "details": {
        "paypal_email": "<string>",
        "wise_email": "<string>",
        "wallet_address": "<string>",
        "crypto_currency": "<string>",
        "bank_country": "AD",
        "account_holder_name": "<string>",
        "account_number": "<string>",
        "routing_aba_number": "<string>",
        "country": "<string>",
        "state": "<string>",
        "postal_code": "<string>",
        "address": "<string>",
        "city": "<string>",
        "transit_number": "<string>",
        "institution_number": "<string>",
        "bsb_code": "<string>",
        "sort_code": "<string>",
        "iban": "<string>",
        "swift_bic_code": "<string>",
        "bank_name": "<string>",
        "bank_city": "<string>",
        "bank_address": "<string>"
      },
      "method": "paypal",
      "is_disabled": true,
      "is_selected": true
    }
    '

#### Authorizations

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-affiliate/payout-methods/update-a-payout-method#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Access token passed as a Bearer token in the Authorization header

#### Headers

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-affiliate/payout-methods/update-a-payout-method#parameter-account-id)

Account-ID

string

required

Account identifier that specifies which account is making the request

Example:

`"acc_123456"`

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-affiliate/payout-methods/update-a-payout-method#parameter-id)

Create promo code

cURL

Copy

    curl --request POST \
      --url https://api.firstpromoter.com/api/v2/affiliate/promo_codes \
      --header 'Account-ID: <account-id>' \
      --header 'Authorization: Bearer <token>' \
      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      --data '
    {
      "code": "<string>",
      "reward_id": 123,
      "promoter_campaign_id": 123,
      "description": "<string>",
      "metadata": {},
      "details": {}
    }
    '

Update promo code by id

cURL

Copy

    curl --request PUT \
      --url https://api.firstpromoter.com/api/v2/affiliate/promo_codes/{id} \
      --header 'Account-ID: <account-id>' \
      --header 'Authorization: Bearer <token>' \
      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      --data '
    {
      "code": "<string>",
      "description": "<string>",
      "reward_id": 123,
      "promoter_campaign_id": 123,
      "metadata": {},
      "details": {}
    }
    '

# Get chart data - FirstPromoter Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-affiliate/promoters/get-chart-data#content-area)

[FirstPromoter Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/firstpromoter/HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL&q=85&s=6ded212b82547bec37a22e90f72eeb71)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/firstpromoter/HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL&q=85&s=c393ff83772047b8a444f78a1e393e7f)](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/)

[API Reference](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-admin/introduction)
[Affiliate API Reference](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-affiliate/introduction)

Get chart data

cURL

Copy

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://api.firstpromoter.com/api/v2/affiliate/promoters/chart_data \
      --header 'Account-ID: <account-id>' \
      --header 'Authorization: Bearer <token>'

GET

/

promoters

/

chart\_data

Try it

Get chart data

cURL

Copy

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://api.firstpromoter.com/api/v2/affiliate/promoters/chart_data \
      --header 'Account-ID: <account-id>' \
      --header 'Authorization: Bearer <token>'

#### Authorizations

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-affiliate/promoters/get-chart-data#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Access token passed as a Bearer token in the Authorization header

#### Headers

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-affiliate/promoters/get-chart-data#parameter-account-id)

Account-ID

string

required

Account identifier that specifies which account is making the request

Example:

`"acc_123456"`

#### Query Parameters

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-affiliate/promoters/get-chart-data#parameter-promoter-campaign-id)

promoter\_campaign\_id

integer

If provided, the given promoter campaign will be used in chart. Otherwise all the current\_promoter campaigns will be used.

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-affiliate/promoters/get-chart-data#parameter-period-from)

period\_from

string<date>

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-affiliate/promoters/get-chart-data#parameter-period-to)

period\_to

string<date>

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-affiliate/promoters/get-chart-data#parameter-selection)

selection

enum<string>

Available options:

`revenue`,

`commissions`,

`clicks`,

`referrals`,

`customers`,

`cancellations`

#### Response

401

Unauthorized

[Get current promoter sub affiliates](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-affiliate/promoters/get-current-promoter-sub-affiliates)
[Get the promoter email](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-affiliate/promoters/get-the-promoter-email)

‚åòI

Get current promoter

cURL

Copy

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://api.firstpromoter.com/api/v2/affiliate/promoters/current \
      --header 'Account-ID: <account-id>' \
      --header 'Authorization: Bearer <token>'

Copy

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://api.firstpromoter.com/api/v2/affiliate/promoters/sub_affiliates \
      --header 'Account-ID: <account-id>' \
      --header 'Authorization: Bearer <token>'

Set the user password

cURL

Copy

    curl --request PUT \

      --header 'Account-ID: <account-id>' \
      --header 'Authorization: Bearer <token>' \
      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      --data '
    {
      "id": "<string>",
      "user": {
        "new_password": "<string>",
        "new_password_confirmation": "<string>"
      }
    }
    '

# Tracking with fpr.js - FirstPromoter Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/guides/tracking-with-fprjs#content-area)

[FirstPromoter Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/firstpromoter/HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL&q=85&s=6ded212b82547bec37a22e90f72eeb71)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/firstpromoter/HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL&q=85&s=c393ff83772047b8a444f78a1e393e7f)](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/)

v2

Search...

‚åòK

Search...

Navigation

How to guides

Tracking with fpr.js

[Documentation](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/introduction)
[API Reference](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-admin/introduction)

On this page

*   [Installation](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/guides/tracking-with-fprjs#installation)
    
*   [Tracking Flow](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/guides/tracking-with-fprjs#tracking-flow)
    
*   [1\. Click Tracking](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/guides/tracking-with-fprjs#1-click-tracking)
    
*   [2\. Referral Tracking](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/guides/tracking-with-fprjs#2-referral-tracking)
    
*   [3\. Sales Tracking](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/guides/tracking-with-fprjs#3-sales-tracking)
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/guides/tracking-with-fprjs#installation)

Installation
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

First Add the main tracking scripts to your website. Replace `<your-account-id-here>` with your **actual account id** found in the settings > integrations page on your FirstPromoter dashboard.

Copy

    <script>
        (function (w) { w.fpr = w.fpr || function () { w.fpr.q = w.fpr.q || []; w.fpr.q[arguments[0] == 'set' ? 'unshift' : 'push'](arguments); }; })(window);
        fpr("init", { cid: "<your-account-id-here>" });
        fpr("click");
    </script>
    <script src="https://cdn.firstpromoter.com/fpr.js" async></script>
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/guides/tracking-with-fprjs#tracking-flow)

Tracking Flow
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/guides/tracking-with-fprjs#1-click-tracking)

1\. Click Tracking

The main tracking script automatically tracks visitors that come through your affiliate links:

*   When a visitor arrives on your website using a referral link the main tracking script will automatically track the click.
*   The click sets 2 cookies in the browser - `_fprom_ref` and `_fprom_tid`
*   These cookies are used for tracking in future without the need for a referral link.

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/guides/tracking-with-fprjs#2-referral-tracking)

2\. Referral Tracking

When a visitor signs up or fills an opt-in form, convert them to a referral by using the signup function:

Copy

    <script>
      fpr("referral",{email: '[email¬Ýprotected]', uid: '123456'});
    </script>
    

You can send only the email or only the uid or both. You need to ensure that the actual visitor data is passed to the function.

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/guides/tracking-with-fprjs#3-sales-tracking)

3\. Sales Tracking

If you are using [Stripe](https://login.firstpromoter.com/?redirect=%2Fintegration%2Fstripe)
, [Chargebee](https://login.firstpromoter.com/?redirect=%2Fintegration%2Fchargebee)
, [Braintree](https://login.firstpromoter.com/?redirect=%2Fintegration%2Fbraintree)
, [Paddle](https://login.firstpromoter.com/?redirect=%2Fintegration%2Fpaddle)
 or [Recurly](https://login.firstpromoter.com/?redirect=%2Fintegration%2Frecurly)
 we can track sales automatically on our end. You will only need to connect your billing provider to FirstPromoter.

If you use any other billing provider you will need to track sales using the tracking [API](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-admin/tracking-api/sales)
. For more information on sales tracking API, see documentation [here](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-admin/tracking-api/sales)

When a sale event is received, FirstPromoter will automatically:

*   Identify the corresponding affiliate to assign the sale to.
*   Assign the corresponding reward/commission to the promoter.

With this in place you have completed the basic tracking flow. From tracking of clicks through to assigning the corresponding commissions to the affiliates.

[Quickstart](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/quickstart)
[Tracking without fpr.js](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/guides/tracking-without-fprjs)

‚åòI

# How FirstPromoter works - FirstPromoter Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/how-it-works#content-area)

[FirstPromoter Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/firstpromoter/HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL&q=85&s=6ded212b82547bec37a22e90f72eeb71)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/firstpromoter/HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL&q=85&s=c393ff83772047b8a444f78a1e393e7f)](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/)

v2

Search...

‚åòK

Search...

Navigation

Overview

How FirstPromoter works

[Documentation](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/introduction)
[API Reference](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-admin/introduction)

On this page

*   [Setting Up a Campaign](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/how-it-works#setting-up-a-campaign)
    
*   [Click Tracking](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/how-it-works#click-tracking)
    
*   [Referral Tracking](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/how-it-works#referral-tracking)
    
*   [Sales Tracking](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/how-it-works#sales-tracking)
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/how-it-works#setting-up-a-campaign)

Setting Up a Campaign
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Setting up a campaign with FirstPromoter is seamless and can be done in just a few clicks. During the onboarding process, you will create your first campaign. Each campaign generates a unique signup link that can be shared with your affiliates. When they sign up, FirstPromoter creates a unique referral link using the website URL you provide. Affiliates can then share their referral link with potential customers.

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/how-it-works#click-tracking)

Click Tracking
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click tracking on FirstPromoter works after adding the main tracking script to your website. It works only once when a user visits a referral link by sending a `click` event to FirstPromoter.

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/how-it-works#referral-tracking)

Referral Tracking
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Referral tracking occurs when a lead is captured on your website and sent to FirstPromoter after they sign up or fill out a form. This is achieved via the referral tracking script or API, which requires you to send the referral email address or UID to FirstPromoter. When a lead visits with a referral link, two cookies, `_fprom_tid` and `_fprom_ref`are set in their browser. These cookies have a default lifespan of 60 days (adjustable in the Admin panel) and are essential for the referral tracking script to function.

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/how-it-works#sales-tracking)

Sales Tracking
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Sales tracking is crucial for calculating commissions for affiliates. By default, FirstPromoter automatically tracks sales from providers like `Stripe`,`Chargebee`,`Braintree (subscriptions)`,`Recurly`, `Paddle` by listening to and cross-referencing events sent from the billing provider. For other billing providers or custom setups, we provide an API to send sales events to FirstPromoter.

[Introduction](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/introduction)
[Quickstart](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/quickstart)

‚åòI

---

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/guides/tracking-without-fprjs#tracking-flow)

Tracking Flow
================================================================================================

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/guides/tracking-without-fprjs#1-store-and-retrieve-link-token-referral-id-:)

1\. Store and retrieve link token (Referral ID):
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When a visitor arrives through a referral link (e.g., [https://yourdomain.com?fpr=joe13](https://yourdomain.com/?fpr=joe13)
, where `fpr` is the affiliate‚Äôs Referral ID parameter and `joe13` is the value), retrieve the referral link token (Referral ID) from the referral link, store it in the browser‚Äôs localStorage or as cookie for later use.

The available query parameters are `?fpr`, `?via`, `?fp_ref`, `?deal`, `?ref`, `?_from`, `?_by`, `?_go` .

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/guides/tracking-without-fprjs#i-store-referral-link-token-implementation)

I. Store referral link token implementation

client side (localStorage implementation)

client side (cookie implementation)

Copy

    <script>
    // Function to store referral link token in localStorage
    function storeReferralLinkTokenInLocalStorage(referralLinkTokenParam) {
        // Get URL parameters
        const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
        const referralLinkToken = urlParams.get(referralLinkTokenParam.replace("?",""));
    
        if (referralLinkToken) {
            localStorage.setItem('_fprom_ref', referralLinkToken);
        }
         else{
            console.log(`No such query parameter '${referralLinkTokenParam.replace("?","")}' or '${referralLinkTokenParam}' found in ${window.location.search}`);
        }
    }
    
    // Call the function to store the Referral ID/token when the page loads by passing the query parameter.
    
    storeReferralLinkTokenInLocalStorage('fpr');
    </script>
    

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/guides/tracking-without-fprjs#ii-retrive-referral-id/token)

II. Retrive referral ID/token

client-side (localStorage implementation)

client Side(cookie retrieval implementation)

Server Side (cookie retrieval implementation)

Copy

    
    <script>
    // Function to retrieve referral ID/token stored in localStorage
    function getReferralLinkToken() {
        return localStorage.getItem('_fprom_ref');
    }
    
    // Call the `getReferralLinkToken` function whenever you want to get referral ID/token on any of the pages.
    
    var ref_id = getReferralLinkToken();
    </script>
    
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/guides/tracking-without-fprjs#2-lead/referral-tracking)

2\. Lead/Referral tracking
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When a visitor signs up or fills an opt-in form, convert them to a referral by using the [track/signup](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-admin/tracking-api/leads-and-signups)
 endpoint.

You can send only the email or only the uid or both. You need to ensure that the actual visitor data is passed in the API call.

Copy

    curl --request POST \
      --url https://api.firstpromoter.com/api/v2/track/signup \
      --header 'Account-ID: <account-id>' \
      --header 'Authorization: Bearer <token>' \
      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      --data '{
    	  "email": "[email¬Ýprotected]",
    	  "uid": "cus_000001",
    	  "ref_id": "joe13",
    	  "skip_email_notification": true
    }'
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/guides/tracking-without-fprjs#3-sales-tracking)

3\. Sales Tracking
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you are using [Stripe](https://login.firstpromoter.com/?redirect=%2Fintegration%2Fstripe)
, [Chargebee](https://login.firstpromoter.com/?redirect=%2Fintegration%2Fchargebee)
, [Braintree](https://login.firstpromoter.com/?redirect=%2Fintegration%2Fbraintree)
, [Paddle](https://login.firstpromoter.com/?redirect=%2Fintegration%2Fpaddle)
 or [Recurly](https://login.firstpromoter.com/?redirect=%2Fintegration%2Frecurly)
 we can track sales automatically on our end. You will only need to connect your billing provider to FirstPromoter.

If you use any other billing provider you will need to track sales using the tracking [API](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-admin/tracking-api/sales)
. For more information on sales tracking API, see documentation [here](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-admin/tracking-api/sales)

When a sale event is received, FirstPromoter will automatically:

*   Identify the corresponding affiliate to assign the sale to.
*   Assign the corresponding reward/commission to the promoter.

With this in place, you have completed the basic tracking flow. From storing and retrieval of affiliate referral link token (Referral ID) through to assigning the corresponding commissions to the affiliates.

[Tracking with fpr.js](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/guides/tracking-with-fprjs)
[Proxy Setup (Optional)](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/guides/proxy-setup)

# Proxy Setup (Optional) - FirstPromoter Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/guides/proxy-setup#content-area)

[FirstPromoter Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/firstpromoter/HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL&q=85&s=6ded212b82547bec37a22e90f72eeb71)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/firstpromoter/HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL&q=85&s=c393ff83772047b8a444f78a1e393e7f)](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/)

Navigation

How to guides

Proxy Setup (Optional)

[Documentation](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/introduction)
[API Reference](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-admin/introduction)

On this page

*   [Overview](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/guides/proxy-setup#overview)
    
*   [The Challenge with Ad Blockers](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/guides/proxy-setup#the-challenge-with-ad-blockers)
    
*   [Proxy Integration Solution](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/guides/proxy-setup#proxy-integration-solution)
    
*   [Implementation Methods](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/guides/proxy-setup#implementation-methods)
    
*   [Method 1: Vercel redirect setup](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/guides/proxy-setup#method-1%3A-vercel-redirect-setup)
    
*   [Method 2: Cloudflare workers setup](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/guides/proxy-setup#method-2%3A-cloudflare-workers-setup)
    
*   [Method 3: Apache setup](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/guides/proxy-setup#method-3%3A-apache-setup)
    
*   [Method 4: NGINX setup](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/guides/proxy-setup#method-4%3A-nginx-setup)
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/guides/proxy-setup#overview)

Overview
---------------------------------------------------------------------------

This document outlines how to implement proxy integrations with FirstPromoter to ensure reliable tracking even when ad blockers are present. By leveraging a proxy setup, you can maintain accurate affiliate tracking and conversion attribution while minimizing the impact of ad blocking technologies.

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/guides/proxy-setup#the-challenge-with-ad-blockers)

The Challenge with Ad Blockers
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Ad blockers and privacy tools can interfere with affiliate tracking in several ways:

*   Blocking tracking scripts from loading
*   Preventing cookies from being set
*   Blocking HTTP requests to domains identified as tracking services
*   Stripping tracking parameters from URLs

![](https://mintcdn.com/firstpromoter/rNk-Jdvp2vdjAvd9/images/adblocker-l.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=rNk-Jdvp2vdjAvd9&q=85&s=e46d0a6f4ed9ed78a027ff02f2cb7f47) ![](https://mintcdn.com/firstpromoter/rNk-Jdvp2vdjAvd9/images/adblocker-d.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=rNk-Jdvp2vdjAvd9&q=85&s=7d58febc53bd49bae4dde7059593f0cd) FirstPromoter, like many affiliate platforms, can be affected by these measures, resulting in lost attribution data and commission tracking failures.

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/guides/proxy-setup#proxy-integration-solution)

Proxy Integration Solution
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A proxy integration routes tracking requests through your own domain or a custom domain instead of directly to FirstPromoter‚Äôs tracking domain. This approach has several advantages:

*   **Improved Deliverability**: Requests appear to come from your trusted domain, not a third-party tracking service
*   **Reduced Blocking**: Most ad blockers don‚Äôt block first-party requests
*   **Enhanced Privacy**: User data stays within your domain ecosystem
*   **Better Performance**: Removes additional DNS lookups to third-party domains

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/guides/proxy-setup#implementation-methods)

Implementation Methods

#### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/guides/proxy-setup#method-1:-vercel-redirect-setup)

Method 1: Vercel redirect setup

If your service is hosted by Vercel, they provide an option to reroute your requests. To set up a Vercel redirect, follow these steps:

1.  Find your vercel.json file. This is usually in your root directory.
2.  Add the following lines to your vercel.json file:

Copy

    {
        "rewrites": [\
          {\
            "source": "/get_details",\
            "destination": "https://t.firstpromoter.com/get_details"\
          },\
          {\
            "source": "/tr",\
            "destination": "https://t.firstpromoter.com/tr"\
          }\
        ]
      }
    

You can change the source paths to anything that you like. However you will need to update the URL‚Äôs in the tracking scripts as well. For these we provide the following variables which you will use when setting up your scripts : `window.proxy_fpr_tr_url` and `window.proxy_fpr_get_details_url`

3.  Download the tracking scripts from [here (Click here)](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/firstpromoter/docs/refs/heads/main/downloadables/fpr-prox.js)
     and add it to your main websites public directory. This will allow it to be fetched from your website. You can change the name of the file to anything but remember to rename it in the main tracking code below.
4.  For your main tracking scripts, add the following code. Please replace `<your-account-id-here>` with your **actual account id** in the settings > integrations page on your FirstPromoter dashboard. If you changed the urls to something more custom you can uncomment the `window.proxy_fpr_tr_url` and `window.proxy_fpr_get_details_url` variables and update them to match your proxy urls.

Copy

        <script>
           // window.proxy_fpr_tr_url =`/tr`;
           // window.proxy_fpr_get_details_url=`/get_details`
    
            (function (w) { w.fpr = w.fpr || function () { w.fpr.q = w.fpr.q || []; w.fpr.q[arguments[0] == 'set' ? 'unshift' : 'push'](arguments); }; })(window);
            fpr("init", { cid: "<your-account-id-here>" });
            fpr("click");
        </script>
        <script src="/fpr-prox.js" defer async=""></script>
    

6.  Deploy your changes and test using the brave browser or install uBlockOrigin and confirm if your tracking is working as expected

#### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/guides/proxy-setup#method-2:-cloudflare-workers-setup)

Method 2: Cloudflare workers setup

Cloudflare provides a free plan with up to 100,000 requests per day, making it a good choice for a reverse proxy setup. To set up a Cloudflare worker, follow these steps:

1.  Set up a Cloudflare Worker Navigate to the Cloudflare dashboard, select `Compute (Workers)` > `Workers & Pages` > `Create`. You can choose a custom name for your worker or use the default one. Click ‚ÄúDeploy‚Äù when ready.  
    
    Please take note of the url of your worker as this will be needed in your setup of the tracking scripts.
    
2.  Modify the Worker for Proxy Functionality After deploying your new worker, click ‚ÄúEdit code‚Äù. If you‚Äôre already on the worker‚Äôs page, select ‚ÄúQuick edit‚Äù. This will open a code editor where you should replace the existing code with the following proxy code:

Copy

    const FP_CDN_HOST = "https://cdn.firstpromoter.com/fpr-proxy.js";
    const FP_HOST = "https://t.firstpromoter.com";
    
    async function handleRequest(request, ctx) {
      const url = new URL(request.url)
      const pathname = url.pathname
      const search = url.search
      const pathWithParams = pathname + search
      return forwardRequest(request, pathWithParams)
    }
    
    async function forwardRequest(request, pathWithSearch) {
      const originRequest = new Request(request)
      originRequest.headers.delete("cookie")
      return await fetch(`${FP_HOST}${pathWithSearch}`, originRequest)
    }
    
    
    export default {
      async fetch(request, env, ctx) {
        return handleRequest(request, ctx);
      }
    };
    

3.  When done, click ‚ÄúSave and deploy‚Äù.
4.  Download the tracking scripts from [here (Click here)](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/firstpromoter/docs/refs/heads/main/downloadables/fpr-prox.js)
     and add it to your main websites public directory. This will allow it to be fetched from your website. You can change the name of the file to anything but remember to rename it in the main tracking code below.
5.  For your main tracking scripts, add the following code. Please replace `<worker-url-here>` with the url of your worker and `<your-account-id-here>` with your **actual account id** in the settings > integrations page on your FirstPromoter dashboard.

Copy

        <script>
            const WORKER_URL = "<worker-url-here>";
            window.proxy_fpr_tr_url =`${WORKER_URL}/tr`;
            window.proxy_fpr_get_details_url=`${WORKER_URL}/get_details`
    
            (function (w) { w.fpr = w.fpr || function () { w.fpr.q = w.fpr.q || []; w.fpr.q[arguments[0] == 'set' ? 'unshift' : 'push'](arguments); }; })(window);
            fpr("init", { cid: "<your-account-id-here>" });
            fpr("click");
        </script>
        <script src="/fpr-prox.js" defer async=""></script>
    

6.  Test using the brave browser or install uBlockOrigin and confirm if your tracking is working as expected

#### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/guides/proxy-setup#method-3:-apache-setup)

Method 3: Apache setup

1.  Find your apache config. Depending on your setup you may need to put the below in your default-ssl.conf file. `yourdomain.com/tr` will be pointed to `https://t.firstpromoter.com/tr` and `yourdomain.com/tr/get_details` will point to `https://t.firstpromoter.com/get_details`.

Feel free to change `/tr` to anything you want on your domain if you do you will be required to set the following in your script `window.proxy_fpr_tr_url` and `window.proxy_fpr_get_details_url`

Copy

    <VirtualHost _default_:443>
    
      #your other configs
    
    	<IfModule mod_proxy.c>
          <IfModule mod_proxy_http.c>
              ProxyPass /tr/get_details https://t.firstpromoter.com/get_details
              ProxyPassReverse /tr/get_details https://t.firstpromoter.com/get_details
              
    		  ProxyPass /tr https://t.firstpromoter.com/tr
              ProxyPassReverse /tr https://t.firstpromoter.com/tr
          </IfModule>
      </IfModule>
    
    </VirtualHost>
    

Feel free to change `/tr` and `/tr/get_details` to anything you want on your domain if you do you will be required to set the following in your script `window.proxy_fpr_tr_url` and `window.proxy_fpr_get_details_url`

2.  Restart your server. `sudo service apache2 restart`
3.  Download the FirstPromoter scripts from [here (Click here)](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/firstpromoter/docs/refs/heads/main/downloadables/fpr-prox.js)
     and add it to your main websites public directory. This will allow it to be fetched from your website.
4.  Add the scripts below directly to your website. Replace `<your-account-id-here>` with your **actual account id** in the settings > integrations page on your FirstPromoter dashboard.

Copy

    
        <script>
            window.proxy_fpr_tr_url ="/tr";
            window.proxy_fpr_get_details_url="/tr/get_details";
            (function (w) { w.fpr = w.fpr || function () { w.fpr.q = w.fpr.q || []; w.fpr.q[arguments[0] == 'set' ? 'unshift' : 'push'](arguments); }; })(window);
            fpr("init", { cid: "<your-account-id-here>" });
            fpr("click");
        </script>
        <script src="/fpr-prox.js" defer async=""></script>
    

5.  Deploy and test using the brave browser or install uBlockOrigin and confirm if your tracking is working as expected.

#### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/guides/proxy-setup#method-4:-nginx-setup)

Method 4: NGINX setup

1.  Find your NGINX config file. This is typically at: `/etc/nginx/sites-available/yourdomain.com` Or if using a default site: `/etc/nginx/sites-available/default`

Then within the server block, add the proxy rules like this:

Copy

    
    location /tr/get_details {
        proxy_pass https://t.firstpromoter.com/get_details;
        proxy_set_header Host t.firstpromoter.com;
        proxy_ssl_server_name on;
    }
    
    location /tr {
        proxy_pass https://t.firstpromoter.com/tr;
        proxy_set_header Host t.firstpromoter.com;
        proxy_ssl_server_name on;
    }
    
    

The contents of your file should look like the below

Copy

    server {
        listen 80;
        server_name yourdomain.com;
    
        location /tr/get_details {
            proxy_pass https://t.firstpromoter.com/get_details;
            proxy_set_header Host t.firstpromoter.com;
            proxy_ssl_server_name on;
        }
    
        location /tr {
            proxy_pass https://t.firstpromoter.com/tr;
            proxy_set_header Host t.firstpromoter.com;
            proxy_ssl_server_name on;
        }
    
        # other configs here
    }
    

2.  Restart your server. `sudo service nginx restart`
3.  Download the FirstPromoter scripts from from [here (Click here)](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/firstpromoter/docs/refs/heads/main/downloadables/fpr-prox.js)
     and add it to your main websites public directory. This will allow it to be fetched from your website.
4.  Add the scripts below directly to your website. Replace `your-account-id-here` with your **actual account id** in the settings > integrations page on your FirstPromoter dashboard.

Copy

    
        <script>
            window.proxy_fpr_tr_url ="/tr";
            window.proxy_fpr_get_details_url="/tr/get_details";
            (function (w) { w.fpr = w.fpr || function () { w.fpr.q = w.fpr.q || []; w.fpr.q[arguments[0] == 'set' ? 'unshift' : 'push'](arguments); }; })(window);
            fpr("init", { cid: "<your-account-id-here>" });
            fpr("click");
        </script>
        <script src="/fpr-prox.js" defer async=""></script>
    

5.  Deploy and test using the brave browser or install uBlockOrigin and confirm if your tracking is working as expected

`Difficulty: Intermediate`  
`Developer Required: Yes` Our API allows you to track sales, refunds, upgrades and cancellations even if you have a billing provider we do not support.

**Precondition**:  
You will need to set up an endpoint on your server for which you will receive webhook events from your billing provider.  
Once you are receiving webhook events on your server from your billing provider, you can then make a request to FirstPromoter to track sales when events are received.

# Introduction - FirstPromoter Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/introduction#content-area)

[FirstPromoter Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/firstpromoter/HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL&q=85&s=6ded212b82547bec37a22e90f72eeb71)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/firstpromoter/HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL&q=85&s=c393ff83772047b8a444f78a1e393e7f)](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/)

v2

[API Reference](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-admin/introduction)

On this page

*   [What is FirstPromoter](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/introduction#what-is-firstpromoter)
    
*   [Benefits of using FirstPromoter](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/introduction#benefits-of-using-firstpromoter)
    
*   [Key Features](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/introduction#key-features)
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/introduction#what-is-firstpromoter)

What is FirstPromoter
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

FirstPromoter is a modern and reliable affiliate tool for subscription-based/SaaS companies that enables you to track, manage and optimize referral-based marketing programs. It is easy to set up, yet powerful to scale with your growing needs. Instead of coding your own affiliate programs, you can simply integrate with FirstPromoter to handle your affiliate programs for you with a few lines of code.

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/introduction#benefits-of-using-firstpromoter)

Benefits of using FirstPromoter

Use your own domain
-------------------

Set your own domain (with SSL encryption support) for affiliate dashboard and sign up pages.

Individual rewards and bonuses
------------------------------

Give performance bonuses and personalize the commissions and rewards scheme for each affiliate individually.

Advanced reporting
------------------

Oversee the performance of your affiliate program across 18 data points.

Fraud protection
----------------

Affiliates get commissions only when the purchase is confirmed by your billing provider. We also have algorithms to identify suspicious leads.

SEO-friendly referral links
---------------------------

No redirects. No ugly short-links. Get the maximum SEO juice with referral links in 8 formats.

Invite your team
----------------

Get your teammates inside FirstPromoter. You can set 4 different user roles ( `Manager`, `Admin`, `Admin Plus`, `Super Admin`) and restrict access to certain campaigns.

Multiple currencies
-------------------

We support 190 currencies and can do conversions in 170. We use daily updated exchange rates and you can apply your own exchange fee.

Custom CSS and JavaScript
-------------------------

Get unlimited flexibility on your affiliates‚Äô dashboard. From enabling services like live-chat, surveys or analytics to changing the design completely.

Embeddable affiliate dashboard
------------------------------

You can embed the affiliate dashboard inside your application and log your users in automatically, without asking them to enter a password or email.

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/introduction#key-features)

Key Features

Launch affiliate and referral campaigns with ease
-------------------------------------------------

Follow the step-by-step setup to start your first affiliate program, no matter how simple or complex your affiliate scheme is.

Customize the affiliate dashboard with your branding
----------------------------------------------------

Edit the affiliate dashboard to make it yours. Add your colors, logo, and choose the layout that suits you.

Track personalized referral links and coupon codes
--------------------------------------------------

Track sales by discount coupon codes alone, email or personalized referral links.

Leverage powerful reporting
---------------------------

Oversee the performance of your affiliate program across 18 data points.

Save time with one-click payouts
--------------------------------

Pay hundreds of affiliates at once, directly from the FirstPromoter dashboard.

[How FirstPromoter works](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/how-it-works)

‚åòI

Custom

Paddle Checkout

[Documentation](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/introduction)
[API Reference](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-admin/introduction)

`Difficulty: Intermediate`  
`Developer Required: Yes`

Depending on the complexity of your website it is ideal to have a developer assist you in the setup.

If you are using the paddle checkout feature on your website you can integrate with FirstPromoter. This setup mainly requires you to add tracking scripts into your website and setting extra configurations on your paddle billing/classic checkout function `Paddle.Checkout.open()` or `Paddle.Initialize()`. Click [here](https://login.firstpromoter.com/?redirect=%2Finstructions%2Fpaddle-checkout)
 to view the guide.

# Google Tag Manager - FirstPromoter Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/integrations/tracking/custom/gtm#content-area)

[FirstPromoter Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/firstpromoter/HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL&q=85&s=6ded212b82547bec37a22e90f72eeb71)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/firstpromoter/HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL&q=85&s=c393ff83772047b8a444f78a1e393e7f)](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/)

v2

Search...

‚åòK

Search...

Navigation

Custom

Google Tag Manager

[Documentation](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/introduction)
[API Reference](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-admin/introduction)

`Difficulty: Intermediate`  
`Developer Required: Yes` With FirstPromoter you can setup click and signup tracking using our Google Tag Manager option. This setup mainly requires you to add tracking scripts into your Google Tag Manager and sending details about the referrals using the script. Depending on the complexity of your website it is ideal to have a developer assist you in the setup.

This procedure assumes you have already Set up GTM to work on your website.

1.  To get started on FirstPromoter:
    *   [Login](https://login.firstpromoter.com/)
         to your admin account.
    *   Navigate to Settings > Integrations > Integrate your website section of your dashboard.
    *   Click on the `Integrate` button.
    *   Click on the `setup` button or click on the `change` link for a new setup instructions.
    *   Under `Custom integration`, select the `JS` option.
    *   Copy the `Main tracking script` under the `JavaScript` tab.
2.  Login in Google Tag Manager:
    
    *   Navigate to your `Tags` section
    *   Click on `New` button (at top right corner)
    
    ![](https://mintcdn.com/firstpromoter/rNk-Jdvp2vdjAvd9/images/gtm/image-1.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=rNk-Jdvp2vdjAvd9&q=85&s=e412e99024f84938f119aea9d2de9074)
    
    *   Click on the `Tag configuration` panel to open the TAG type selection panel.
    
    ![](https://mintcdn.com/firstpromoter/rNk-Jdvp2vdjAvd9/images/gtm/image-2.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=rNk-Jdvp2vdjAvd9&q=85&s=a4ed5e7b8c4ec9a2216433b7de59dfce)
    *   Scroll down and select the `Custom HTML` option ![](https://mintcdn.com/firstpromoter/rNk-Jdvp2vdjAvd9/images/gtm/image-3.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=rNk-Jdvp2vdjAvd9&q=85&s=0118f7d7d31837182c272b77f1fc0364)
    *   Add/paste the `Main tracking script` copied from FirstPromoter into the `HTML` Section. As shown in the screenshot below: ![](https://mintcdn.com/firstpromoter/rNk-Jdvp2vdjAvd9/images/gtm/image-4.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=rNk-Jdvp2vdjAvd9&q=85&s=d77f760c6ae940e27a1032d66836ad03)
    *   Now, you need to select when Google Tag Manager should trigger the script. To do this, scroll down to the `triggering` section, click on it and choose when to trigger the tag.
        
        We recommend selecting the `pages trigger` to load the `Main tracking script` on all your landing pages.
        
        ![](https://mintcdn.com/firstpromoter/rNk-Jdvp2vdjAvd9/images/gtm/image-5.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=rNk-Jdvp2vdjAvd9&q=85&s=8291a0efe4329823d7aa9a8a981c45f3) ![](https://mintcdn.com/firstpromoter/HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL/images/gtm/image-5a.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL&q=85&s=c1d3519c4f60516fe8adb79532d9e5f5)
    *   Rename/change the name to `Firstpromoter Main Tracking script` ![](https://mintcdn.com/firstpromoter/HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL/images/gtm/image-6.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL&q=85&s=93e16dcb74a43a69c9d591805a88fee5)
    *   Save and publish your changes. ![](https://mintcdn.com/firstpromoter/HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL/images/gtm/image-7.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL&q=85&s=415e80010ae6f8bad8a107d7f014e901)

[Paddle Checkout](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/integrations/tracking/custom/paddle-checkout)
[Overview](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/overview)

‚åòI

# Get sub ids report for current promoter - FirstPromoter Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-affiliate/reports/get-sub_ids-report-for-current-promoter#content-area)

[FirstPromoter Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/firstpromoter/HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL&q=85&s=6ded212b82547bec37a22e90f72eeb71)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/firstpromoter/HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL&q=85&s=c393ff83772047b8a444f78a1e393e7f)](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/)

[Affiliate API Reference](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-affiliate/introduction)

Get sub\_ids report

cURL

Copy

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://api.firstpromoter.com/api/v2/affiliate/reports/sub_ids \
      --header 'Account-ID: <account-id>' \
      --header 'Authorization: Bearer <token>'

401

403

422

#### Authorizations

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-affiliate/reports/get-sub_ids-report-for-current-promoter#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Access token passed as a Bearer token in the Authorization header

#### Headers

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-affiliate/reports/get-sub_ids-report-for-current-promoter#parameter-account-id)

Account-ID

string

required

Account identifier that specifies which account is making the request

Example:

`"acc_123456"`

#### Query Parameters

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-affiliate/reports/get-sub_ids-report-for-current-promoter#parameter-columns)

columns

enum<string>\[\]

required

Available options:

`clicks_count`,

`revenue_amount`,

`promoter_earnings_amount`,

`referrals_count`,

`customers_count`,

`sales_count`,

`refunds_count`,

`cancelled_customers_count`,

`referrals_to_customers_cr`,

`clicks_to_customers_cr`,

`clicks_to_referrals_cr`

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-affiliate/reports/get-sub_ids-report-for-current-promoter#parameter-q)

q

string

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-affiliate/reports/get-sub_ids-report-for-current-promoter#parameter-group-by)

group\_by

enum<string>

required

Available options:

`day`,

`week`,

`month`,

`year`

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-affiliate/reports/get-sub_ids-report-for-current-promoter#parameter-start-date)

start\_date

string<date-time>

required

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-affiliate/reports/get-sub_ids-report-for-current-promoter#parameter-end-date)

end\_date

string<date-time>

required

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-affiliate/reports/get-sub_ids-report-for-current-promoter#parameter-sorting)

sorting

object

Show child attributes

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-affiliate/reports/get-sub_ids-report-for-current-promoter#parameter-additional-properties)

sorting.{key}

enum<string>

Available options:

`asc`,

`desc`

#### Response

200

application/json

Successful response

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-affiliate/reports/get-sub_ids-report-for-current-promoter#response-items-sub-id)

sub\_id

string

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-affiliate/reports/get-sub_ids-report-for-current-promoter#response-items-id)

id

string

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-affiliate/reports/get-sub_ids-report-for-current-promoter#response-items-data)

data

object

# Concepts & Key Terminologies - FirstPromoter Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/concepts#content-area)

[FirstPromoter Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/firstpromoter/HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL&q=85&s=6ded212b82547bec37a22e90f72eeb71)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/firstpromoter/HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL&q=85&s=c393ff83772047b8a444f78a1e393e7f)](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/)

v2

Search...

‚åòK

Search...

Navigation

Scripts

Concepts & Key Terminologies

[Documentation](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/introduction)
[API Reference](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-admin/introduction)

On this page

*   [Promoter](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/concepts#promoter)
    
*   [Clicks](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/concepts#clicks)
    
*   [Referral](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/concepts#referral)
    
*   [Lead](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/concepts#lead)
    
*   [Customer](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/concepts#customer)
    
*   [Sale](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/concepts#sale)
    
*   [Referral Tracking](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/concepts#referral-tracking)
    
*   [Sale Tracking](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/concepts#sale-tracking)
    
*   [ref\_id](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/concepts#ref-id)
    
*   [tid](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/concepts#tid)
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/concepts#promoter)

Promoter
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

Promoters/Affiliates are individuals or companies who drive traffic to a company‚Äôs website, products, or services through referral links and earn a commission when that traffic converts.

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/concepts#clicks)

Clicks
-------------------------------------------------------------------------

Clicks are the number of unique visits to your website via the referral link. **NB:** The user‚Äôs first click on your website via the referral link is what is counted.

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/concepts#referral)

Referral
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

A referral is an individual or business that signs up for or purchases a service using a referral link. A referral can either be a lead or a customer.

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/concepts#lead)

Lead
---------------------------------------------------------------------

A lead is an individual or business that signs up on your website using a referral link but hasn‚Äôt purchased from your website.

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/concepts#customer)

Customer
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

A customer is an individual or business that signed up on your website using a referral link and has made at least one purchase from your website.

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/concepts#sale)

Sale
---------------------------------------------------------------------

A sale occurs when a customer makes a purchase using a referral link. We generate rewards or commissions only for sales.

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/concepts#referral-tracking)

Referral Tracking
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This refers to when the referral details (email address/UID) are sent to FirstPromoter from your website after they sign up or fill out a form. This can be done using the referral tracking script or API.

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/concepts#sale-tracking)

Sale Tracking
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This refers to when payments are tracked from your billing provider, allowing commissions to be generated for your affiliates.

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/concepts#ref-id)

ref\_id
--------------------------------------------------------------------------

This is the referral id/token assigned to an affiliate/promoter once they signup or are added to a campaign. It is generated by FirstPromoter by default and can be set using our API as well. If a referral link is used it is set as a cookie `_fprom_ref` in your browser

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/concepts#tid)

tid
-------------------------------------------------------------------

This is a tracking ID that is dynamically generated by FirstPromoter when someone visits a referral link. This ID is set as a cookie called `_fprom_tid` in your browser.

[Advanced use cases & examples](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/advanced)
[Stripe](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/integrations/billing/stripe)

‚åòI

---

This setup mainly requires you to add/insert our ready made scripts into your Thinkific website platform. Click [here](https://login.firstpromoter.com/?redirect=%2Finstructions%2Fthinkific)
 to view the guide.

[Kickpages](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/integrations/tracking/platform/kickpages)
[Drop-in Scripts](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/integrations/tracking/platform/chargebee/drop-in-scripts)

# Quickstart - FirstPromoter Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/quickstart#content-area)

[FirstPromoter Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/firstpromoter/HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL&q=85&s=6ded212b82547bec37a22e90f72eeb71)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/firstpromoter/HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL&q=85&s=c393ff83772047b8a444f78a1e393e7f)](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/)

v2

Search...

‚åòK

Search...

Navigation

Overview

Quickstart

[Documentation](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/introduction)
[API Reference](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-admin/introduction)

On this page

*   [Steps](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/quickstart#steps)
    

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/quickstart#steps)

Steps

1

Create an account

[Click here](https://new.firstpromoter.com/company/signup)
 to create an Admin account. If you already have an account, [Login here](https://login.firstpromoter.com/)

If you are a new user, you will need to complete the onboarding process, which involves creating a campaign, connecting your billing provider, and integrating your website.

2

Integrate your billing provider

Connect your billing provider to FirstPromoter. This will enable FirstPromoter to automatically track sales, refunds, upgrades or upsells and cancellations data/record from any of the [supported billing providers](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/integrations/billing)
.  

**NB:** For a billing provider that is not supported by default, there is an option to use our [API](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/integrations/billing/api)

3

Integrate your website

Install or add our ready-made scripts/pixels to your website or [platform](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/integrations/tracking/platform)
. We also provide [universal scripts and an API for custom built websites or apps](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/integrations/tracking/custom)
.

Integrating the tracking script into your website enables you to track clicks and referrals (thus, it allows you to send the lead‚Äôs or referral‚Äôs details such as the `email` or `uid` to FirstPromoter).  
When combined with the billing provider integration, this setup enables FirstPromoter to track sales by linking referral information with transaction data from your billing provider.[Learn more about our tracking script here](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/fpr-js-docs)

You can also track sales using `Coupon Codes`. This option is available for users who want `No-Code` or `No-Scripts` integration or want an alternative to traditional referral links . [Learn more](https://help.firstpromoter.com/en/articles/8971002-how-to-track-sales-with-coupon-codes-in-firstpromoter)

4

Test your integrations

Test all parts of your integration to make sure everything is tracking.

*   Clicks tracking
*   Referral tracking
*   Sales tracking

[How FirstPromoter works](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/how-it-works)
[Tracking with fpr.js](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/guides/tracking-with-fprjs)

‚åòI

---

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/fpr-js-docs#including-fpr-js)

Including fpr.js
================================================================================================

On your FirstPromoter dashboard, under the Settings> Integrations> Integrate your website section, based on the selections you make, you are provided with some scripts which are to be added to your website.

It is ideal that the script is added globally on the HEAD section of every marketing or public page of your website.

Copy

    <script>(function(w){w.fpr=w.fpr||function(){w.fpr.q = w.fpr.q||[];w.fpr.q[arguments[0]=='set'?'unshift':'push'](arguments);};})(window);
    fpr("init", {cid:"xxxxxxxx"}); 
    fpr("click");
    </script>
    <script src="https://cdn.firstpromoter.com/fpr.js" async></script>
    

For JavaScript frameworks, you can simply insert the script on the public index.html page so it will be available when the framework loads. For WordPress websites, you can add the scripts to your header.php file before the closing head tag. To get the best performance, it is ideal that you have the scripts added to all the pages where you need tracking to take place. Also, the Scripts are loaded asynchronously and will not affect the website loading speed.

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/fpr-js-docs#functions)

Functions
==================================================================================

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/fpr-js-docs#fpr-%E2%80%9Cinit%E2%80%9D,options,-callback)

fpr(‚Äúinit‚Äù,options, callback?)
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This method helps initializes FirstPromoter with the provided options. Most of these options are loaded automatically when the script loads, but they can be overwritten by passing different ones to the method. The most used one is ‚Äúref\_id‚Äù which forces the script to track a specific promoter.

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/fpr-js-docs#parameters)

Parameters

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/fpr-js-docs#param-options)

options

object

required

#### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/fpr-js-docs#available-keys)

Available keys

| Property | Description |
| --- | --- |
| cid | FirstPromoter Company Id (required) |
| ref\_id | Referral id/token of the promoter |
| tid | Tracking ID, value stored in fprom\_tid cookie |
| url | Current URL |
| domain | Current domain |
| referrer | Browser referrer/ domain of the previous visited website |

Setting properties that are not in the list above will be ignored.

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/fpr-js-docs#param-callback)

callback

function

A function that will be called after the init function is triggered.

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/fpr-js-docs#fpr-%E2%80%9Cclick%E2%80%9D,payload,-callback)

fpr(‚Äúclick‚Äù,payload?, callback?)
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This method is responsible for click tracking.

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/fpr-js-docs#parameters-2)

Parameters

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/fpr-js-docs#param-payload)

payload

object

This overwrites the stored data exactly like the fpr(‚Äúinit‚Äù‚Ä¶) function does before tracking the click.

#### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/fpr-js-docs#available-keys-2)

Available keys

| Property | Description |
| --- | --- |
| cid | FirstPromoter Company Id |
| ref\_id | Referral id/token of the promoter |
| tid | Tracking ID, value stored in fprom\_tid cookie |
| url | Current URL |
| domain | Current domain |
| referrer | Browser referrer/ domain of the previous visited website |

Setting properties that are not in the list above will be ignored.

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/fpr-js-docs#param-callback-1)

callback

function

The callback function receives the response data object and can then be extracted and use

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/fpr-js-docs#example)

Example

click

click\_with\_referral\_id

Copy

    fpr("click")
    

* * *

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/fpr-js-docs#fpr-%E2%80%9Conready%E2%80%9D,callback)

fpr(‚ÄúonReady‚Äù,callback)
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This method checks if the tracking script is initialized and fully loaded on the page.

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/fpr-js-docs#parameters-3)

Parameters

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/fpr-js-docs#param-callback-2)

callback

function

The callback function receives the response data object and can then be extracted and use

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/fpr-js-docs#example-2)

Example

click

Copy

    fpr("onReady", function(data){
        console.log(data)
    })
    

* * *

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/fpr-js-docs#fpr-%E2%80%9Creferral%E2%80%9D,payload,-callback)

fpr(‚Äúreferral‚Äù,payload, callback?)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This method is used primarily to send the referral details to FirstPromoter. It takes as its payload the email of the referral/lead

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/fpr-js-docs#parameters-4)

Parameters

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/fpr-js-docs#param-payload-1)

payload

object

required

The callback function receives the response data object and can then be extracted and use

#### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/fpr-js-docs#available-keys-3)

Available keys

| Property | Description |
| --- | --- |
| email | actual email of the user |
| uid | user id of the user |

Setting properties that are not in the list above will be ignored.

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/fpr-js-docs#example-3)

Example

referral

referral\_with\_callback

Copy

        fpr('referral',{email:actual_user_email@email.com, uid: 123456})
    

* * *

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/fpr-js-docs#fpr-%E2%80%9Cdetails%E2%80%9D,callback)

fpr(‚Äúdetails‚Äù,callback)
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This method is used in getting the details of the promotion and the promoter. **To avoid making multiple requests, it is important to note that the details are stored in a cookie called ‚Äúfprom\_details‚Äù and is available for a day.**

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/fpr-js-docs#parameters-5)

Parameters

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/fpr-js-docs#param-callback-3)

callback

function

The callback function receives the response data object and can then be extracted and use

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/fpr-js-docs#response-format)

Response Format

Copy

    {
          ref_id: 
          promo_code: 
          campaign_id: 
          customer_promo_code: 
          offer:  
          promoter: {
            id:  
            first_name:  
            last_name:  
          }
    }
    

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/fpr-js-docs#example-4)

Example

click

Copy

    fpr("details", function(data){
        console.log(data)
    })
    

* * *

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/fpr-js-docs#fpr-%E2%80%9Ccrossdomain%E2%80%9D,domains)

fpr(‚ÄúcrossDomain‚Äù,domains)
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This method is used when attempting to track across multiple domains. It mainly appends the tracking details to all links to the domain provided. Note: this works with only direct links and should be added preferably to the footer section or called when the whole page is loaded

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/fpr-js-docs#param-domains)

domains

string|array

The crossDomain(s) you want to track

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/fpr-js-docs#example-5)

Example

one domain

multiple domains

Copy

    fpr('crossDomain','newwebsite.com')
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/fpr-js-docs#fpr-%E2%80%9Curltracking%E2%80%9D)

fpr(‚ÄúurlTracking‚Äù)
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This method is used for Direct URL tracking, thus, if you have landing pages for your affiliates/promoters, you can use the method on those pages if you don‚Äôt want the affiliates/promoters ‚ÄúReferral ID‚Äù to be part of their referral links. For this method to work, you will have to first add FirstPromoter‚Äôs main tracking scripts to the landing page(s) and also enable ‚ÄúDirect URL tracking‚Äù on FirstPromoter. To do so, please check out this article: [How to enable direct URL tracking in FirstPromoter](https://help.firstpromoter.com/en/articles/8971394-how-to-enable-direct-url-tracking-in-firstpromoter)

Please note that the method **should not** be used on your homepage, but instead should only be used on all landing pages of your affiliates/promoters.

Copy

    <script type="text/javascript">
    _fprom=window._fprom||[];window._fprom=_fprom;_fprom.push(["url_tracking",true]);
    if (window.$FPROM){$FPROM.trackVisitor({url_tracking: true})} else if(window.fpr) fpr("urlTracking");
    </script>
    

[Proxy Setup (Optional)](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/guides/proxy-setup)
[Advanced use cases & examples](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/advanced)

‚åòI

# Overview - FirstPromoter Docs

[FirstPromoter Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/firstpromoter/HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL&q=85&s=6ded212b82547bec37a22e90f72eeb71)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/firstpromoter/HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=HBqmI3s-Wsq4TZSL&q=85&s=c393ff83772047b8a444f78a1e393e7f)](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/)

Webhooks

Overview

[Documentation](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/introduction)
[API Reference](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/api-reference-v2/api-admin/introduction)

On this page

*   [Receive FirstPromoter events in your webhook endpoint](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/overview#receive-firstpromoter-events-in-your-webhook-endpoint)

*   [How to set it up](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/overview#how-to-set-it-up)

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/overview#receive-firstpromoter-events-in-your-webhook-endpoint)

Receive FirstPromoter events in your webhook endpoint
====================================================================================================================================================================

Listen to events in your FirstPromoter account on your webhook endpoint so you can use them in your app.

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/overview#why-webhooks)

Why webhooks
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After setting up your FirstPromoter account, you may want to receive events from FirstPromoter in order to trigger an action or automate a process in your application. Webhooks allow you to do this. To receive webhook events, you need to have an endpoint in your application that will accept the event. If you are using a tool like [Zapier](https://zapier.com/)
, [Albato](https://albato.com/apps/firstpromoter)
 or [Make](https://www.make.com/en/integrations/firstpromoter)
 they provide these endpoints when creating an automation flow. After you add the webhook to FirstPromoter, it can push real-time event data to your endpoint when events occur in your FirstPromoter account.

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/overview#how-to-set-it-up)

How to set it up
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Navigate to your Settings page > Select Integrations> Scroll down to the webhooks section. You can also click [here](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/'https://login.firstpromoter.com?redirect=%settings%2Fintegrations%27)
 to go there directly.

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/overview#availible-webhook-events)

Availible webhook events
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Lead Signup
*   Promoter Accepted
*   Reward Created
*   New customer
*   Fulfilment Pending

[Google Tag Manager](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/integrations/tracking/custom/gtm)
[Lead Signup](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/lead-signup)
