[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/advanced#passing-the-ref-id-programmatically)

Passing the ref id programmatically
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`fpr("init",{cid:"...",ref_id:"..."})` Getting the ref id from the url and passing it to fpr init

Custom query parameter

Custom hash

Copy

    <script>(function (w) { w.fpr = w.fpr || function () { w.fpr.q = w.fpr.q || []; w.fpr.q[arguments[0] == 'set' ? 'unshift' : 'push'](arguments); }; })(window);
    
      function getQueryParameter(qParam) {
        var searchParams = new URL(document.location.toString()).searchParams;
        if (searchParams.has(qParam)) {
          return searchParams.get(qParam);
        } else {
          return null;
        }
      }
    
      var customRefValue = getQueryParameter("aff");
      if (customRefValue) {
        fpr("init", { ref_id: customRefValue, cid: "xxxxxx" });
      } else {
        fpr("init", { cid: "xxxxxxx" });
      }
    </script>
    <script src="https://cdn.firstpromoter.com/fpr.js" async></script>
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/advanced#passing-the-ref-id-programmatically-from-a-query-string)

Passing the ref id programmatically from a query string
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

    <script>(function(w){w.fpr=w.fpr||function(){w.fpr.q = w.fpr.q||[];w.fpr.q[arguments[0]=='set'?'unshift':'push'](arguments);};})(window);
    function getParam(param) {
    return new URLSearchParams(window.location.search).get(param);
    }
    var ref_id = getParam("sa");
    if (ref_id) {
    fpr("init", { ref_id, cid: "xxxxxx" });
    } else {
    fpr("init", { cid: "xxxxxx" });
    }
    fpr("click");
    </script>
    <script src="https://cdn.firstpromoter.com/fpr.js" async></script>
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/advanced#forcing-a-new-tid-to-be-created-or-reinitializing-the-firstpromoter-cookies)

Forcing a new tid to be created or reinitializing the FirstPromoter cookies
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can force a new tid to be created by invalidating the old one this can be done by passing cookie\_ref\_id: ‚Äòxxx‚Äô as shown in the example below

Copy

    fpr("referral",{email: getParam("wj_lead_email")}, function(){
    window.fpr("click",{cookie_ref_id: 'xxx'});
    });
    

it can also be used to force new emails to be collected on page refresh

Copy

    <script>(function(w){w.fpr=w.fpr||function(){w.fpr.q = w.fpr.q||[];w.fpr.q[arguments[0]=='set'?'unshift':'push'](arguments);};})(window);
    fpr("init", {cid:"‚Ä¶"});
    fpr("click",{cookie_ref_id: 'xxx'});
    </script>
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/advanced#setting-a-default-promoter)

Setting a default Promoter
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

    <script>
      function getParam(param) {
        return new URLSearchParams(window.location.search).get(param);
      }
    
      (function (w) {w.fpr = w.fpr || function () {w.fpr.q = w.fpr.q || []; w.fpr.q[arguments[0] == 'set' ? 'unshift' : 'push'](arguments);};})(window);
      var hasTid = document.cookie.indexOf('fprom_tid=') > 0;
      var hasRefId = document.cookie.indexOf('fprom_ref=') > 0;
    
      if ((!hasRefId || !hasTid) && !getParam('fpr')) {
        var ref_id = "pm";
        fpr("init", {ref_id, cid: "xxxxxx"});
      } else {
        fpr("init", {cid: "xxxxxx"});
      }
      fpr("click");
    
    </script>
    
    <script src="https://cdn.firstpromoter.com/fpr.js" async></script>
    

[FirstPromoter JavaScript Library (fpr.js)](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/fpr-js-docs)
[Concepts & Key Terminologies](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/script-docs/concepts)

‚åòI

This webhook will be fired right after the reward is attributed. To utilize the ‚Äòfulfilment\_pending‚Äô webhook in FirstPromoter, follow these steps:

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/fulfilment-pending#how-to-respond-to-this-webhook-call:)

How to respond to this webhook call:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Respond with status 200 if you fulfilled the reward on your end. Respond with a 2xx status (except 200) to keep the fulfilment marked as pending on FirstPromoter‚Äôs end. Respond with any other status to indicate an error (FirstPromoter will retry for 7 times during the day).

By setting up a webhook, your endpoint will receive an event when a lead becomes a customer.

This event is triggered only once on the first payment made by the lead.

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/new-customer#response-paramerters)

Response Paramerters
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/new-customer#param-event)

Event

Event Object

Show properties

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/new-customer#param-id)

id

string

The Id of the event

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/new-customer#param-type)

type

string

Indicates the webhook event type, such as `lead_becomes_referral`.

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/new-customer#param-created-at)

created\_at

string

Timestamp of when the event occurred.

default\_promo\_code

string

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/new-customer#param-current-target-reward)

By setting up a webhook, your endpoint will receive an event when a lead signs up.

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/lead-signup#response-paramerters)

Response Paramerters
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/lead-signup#param-event)

Event

Event Object

Show properties

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/lead-signup#param-id)

id

string

The Id of the event

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/lead-signup#param-type)

type

string

Indicates the webhook event type, such as `lead_signup`.

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/lead-signup#param-created-at)

created\_at

string

Timestamp of when the event occurred.

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/lead-signup#param-data)

Data

Data Object

Show properties

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/lead-signup#param-id-1)

id

number

The Id of the lead

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/lead-signup#param-status)

status

string

The state of the lead

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/lead-signup#param-email)

email

string

The email of the lead

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/lead-signup#param-uid)

uid

string

The user id of the lead

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/lead-signup#param-customer-since)

customer\_since

string

The date and time the lead became a customer

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/lead-signup#param-cancelled-at)

cancelled\_at

string

The date and time the lead was cancelled

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/lead-signup#param-plan-name)

plan\_name

string

The plan name the lead is subscribed to

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/lead-signup#param-suspicion)

suspicion

string

This states if the addition of the lead is suspected to be fraudulent

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/lead-signup#param-username)

username

string

The username of the lead

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/lead-signup#param-website)

website

string

The website of the lead

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/lead-signup#param-created-at-1)

created\_at

string

The date and time the lead was created

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/lead-signup#param-split-promotion-id)

split\_promotion\_id

number

The split promotion id of the lead

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/lead-signup#param-split-percentage-value)

split\_percentage\_value

number

The split percentage value of the lead

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/lead-signup#param-promoter)

promoter

Promoter Object

Show properties

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/lead-signup#param-id-2)

id

number

The Id of the promoter

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/lead-signup#param-status-1)

status

string

The status of the promoter

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/lead-signup#param-cust-id)

cust\_id

string

The customer id of the promoter

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/lead-signup#param-email-1)

email

By setting up a webhook, your endpoint will receive an event when a promoter is created.

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/promoter-accepted#response-paramerters)

Response Paramerters

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/promoter-accepted#param-event)

Event

Event Object

Show properties

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/promoter-accepted#param-id)

id

string

The Id of the event

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/promoter-accepted#param-type)

type

string

Indicates the webhook event type, such as `promoter_accepted`.

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/promoter-accepted#param-created-at)

created\_at

string

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/promoter-accepted#param-hidden)

hidden

boolean

Whether the campaign is hidden

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/promoter-accepted#param-visitors-count)

visitors\_count

number

The number of visitors

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/promoter-accepted#param-leads-count)

leads\_count

number

The number of leads

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/promoter-accepted#param-customers-count)

customers\_count

number

The number of customers

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/promoter-accepted#param-refunds-count)

refunds\_count

number

The number of refunds

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/promoter-accepted#param-cancellations-count)

cancellations\_count

number

The number of cancellations

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/promoter-accepted#param-sales-count)

sales\_count

number

The number of sales

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/promoter-accepted#param-sales-total)

sales\_total

number

The total sales

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/promoter-accepted#param-refunds-total)

refunds\_total

number

The total refunds

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/promoter-accepted#param-active-customers-count)

active\_customers\_count

number

The number of active customers

By setting up a webhook, your endpoint will receive an event when a reward is generated.

This event is triggered anytime a reward is generated.

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/reward-created#response-paramerters)

[‚Äã](https://docs.firstpromoter.com/webhooks/reward-created#param-event)

string
